CREATE TABLE IrrigationSystem (system_id INT PRIMARY KEY, system_type VARCHAR(255), capacity FLOAT, field_id INT, FOREIGN KEY (field_id) REFERENCES Field(field_id))

CREATE TABLE Field (field_id INT PRIMARY KEY, field_name VARCHAR(255), area FLOAT, soil_type VARCHAR(255), crop_id INT, FOREIGN KEY (crop_id) REFERENCES Crop(crop_id))

CREATE TABLE CropHealth (health_id INT PRIMARY KEY, health_status VARCHAR(255), timestamp TIMESTAMP, field_id INT, FOREIGN KEY (field_id) REFERENCES Field(field_id))</t><s>GRANT SELECT, INSERT ON Field TO user2</s>

CREATE TABLE WeatherSensor (sensor_id INT PRIMARY KEY, location VARCHAR(255), sensor_type VARCHAR(255), field_id INT, FOREIGN KEY (field_id) REFERENCES Field(field_id))

CREATE TABLE Field (field_id INT PRIMARY KEY, field_name VARCHAR(255), area FLOAT, soil_type VARCHAR(255), crop_id INT, FOREIGN KEY (crop_id) REFERENCES Crop(crop_id))

CREATE TABLE Crop (crop_id INT PRIMARY KEY, crop_name VARCHAR(255), crop_type VARCHAR(255), plant_date DATE, harvest_date DATE)</t><s>grant select, update on weathersensor to user3</s>
